
  
create or replace PROCEDURE BRF37A_DETAIL_PROCEDURE (REPORT_DATE DATE)
IS
  V_REPORT_DATE DATE := To_date (REPORT_DATE, 'DD-MM-YYYY'); 
   V_FROM_DATE dATE :=  ADD_MONTHS (LAST_DAY (REPORT_DATE), -1) + 1;
BEGIN


delete from BRF37A_DETAILTABLE where report_date = V_REPORT_DATE;
Commit;


insert into BRF37A_DETAILTABLE
( foracid, cust_id, ACCT_NAME,REPORT_DATE,ACT_BALANCE_AMT_LC, REPORT_LABLE_1,REPORT_NAME_1)
SELECT  foracid, cust_id, ACCT_NAME,REPORT_DATE,ACT_BALANCE_AMT_LC,REPORT_LABLE_1,REPORT_NAME_1 FROM 
brf37A_mapping_table where report_date = '30-JUN-2023' ;


COMMIT;


END;

create or replace PROCEDURE "BRF37A_MAPPING_PROCEDUURE" (REPORT_DATE VARCHAR2)
 
IS
 
  V_REPORT_DATE DATE := To_date (REPORT_DATE, 'DD-MM-YYYY');

   V_FROM_DATE dATE :=  ADD_MONTHS (LAST_DAY (REPORT_DATE), -1) + 1;

BEGIN



--INSERT VALUES



insert into BRF37A_MAPPING_TABLE
( foracid, cust_id, ACCT_NAME,GL_SUB_HEAD_CODE, SCHM_CODE,NRE_STATUS,ACCT_CRNCY_CODE,REPORT_DATE,
ACT_BALANCE_AMT_LC,SOL_ID,CUST_TYPE,CONSTITUTION_CODE,LEGAL_ENTITY_TYPE)

SOL_ID,CUST_TYPE_CODE_2,CONSTITUTION_CODE,LEGAL_ENTITY_TYPE
FROM GENERAL_MASTER_TABLE where report_date = '30-JUN-2023' AND  constitution_code in ('11501','11502','11503','11504','11505','11506','11509','11599','11601','11602','11603','11604','11605','11606','11607','11608','11699','22101','22201',

  'SPC','TRUST','ULTCO','DMCC','CC','SPLLC','SA','ESTB','REAL','','GOENT','GOVCO','GOVT')
  and GL_SUB_HEAD_CODE in ('13101','13201', '13206', '13215', '13216', '13217', '13220','13241', '24301', '24311','24312', '24313', '24319', '24503','24337','13222')
  and SCHM_CODE IN ('CA101','CA102','CA103','CA106','CA107','CA108','CA109','CA110','CA111','CA112','LA101','LA106','OD001','OD002','OD003','OD028','OD651','SB105','SB107',
'TD115') AND ACT_BALANCE_AMT_LC>=0 ;

( foracid, cust_id, ACCT_NAME,GL_SUB_HEAD_CODE, SCHM_CODE,NRE_STATUS,ACCT_CRNCY_CODE,REPORT_DATE,
ACT_BALANCE_AMT_LC,SOL_ID,CUST_TYPE,CONSTITUTION_CODE,LEGAL_ENTITY_TYPE)

SOL_ID,CUST_TYPE_CODE_2,CONSTITUTION_CODE,LEGAL_ENTITY_TYPE
FROM GENERAL_MASTER_TABLE where report_date = '30-JUN-2023' AND BACID IN ('13201001','13246001','13291001') ;

insert into BRF37A_MAPPING_TABLE
( foracid, cust_id, ACCT_NAME,GL_SUB_HEAD_CODE, SCHM_CODE,NRE_STATUS,ACCT_CRNCY_CODE,REPORT_DATE,
ACT_BALANCE_AMT_LC,SOL_ID,CUST_TYPE,CONSTITUTION_CODE,LEGAL_ENTITY_TYPE)
SELECT  ACCT_NUMBER, cust_id, ACCT_NAME,GL_SUB_HEAD_CODE, SCHM_CODE,NRE_FLG,ACCT_CRNCY_CODE,REPORT_DATE,ACT_BALANCE_AMT_LC,
SOL_ID,CUST_TYPE_CODE_2,CONSTITUTION_CODE,LEGAL_ENTITY_TYPE
FROM GENERAL_MASTER_TABLE where report_date = '30-JUN-2023' AND constitution_code in ('44101','44102','44103','44104','44105','44106','44107','44108','44109',
  '44110','44111','44112','44113','44114','44115','44116','44199','44201','44202','44203','44204','44205','44206','44207','44208','44209',
  '44210','44211','44212','44213','44214','44215','44216', '44217', '44299','71005','INDL','INDL ','INDVF','INDVM','NREIN','WPS','RESIN')
  and GL_SUB_HEAD_CODE in ('13101','13201', '13206', '13215', '13216', '13217', '13220','13241', '24301', '24311','24312', '24313', '24319', '24503','24337','13222')

       AND ACT_BALANCE_AMT_LC>=0;
       
       
insert into BRF37A_MAPPING_TABLE
( foracid, cust_id, ACCT_NAME,GL_SUB_HEAD_CODE, SCHM_CODE,NRE_STATUS,ACCT_CRNCY_CODE,REPORT_DATE,
ACT_BALANCE_AMT_LC,SOL_ID,CUST_TYPE,CONSTITUTION_CODE,LEGAL_ENTITY_TYPE)
SELECT  ACCT_NUMBER, cust_id, ACCT_NAME,GL_SUB_HEAD_CODE, SCHM_CODE,NRE_FLG,ACCT_CRNCY_CODE,REPORT_DATE,ACT_BALANCE_AMT_LC,
SOL_ID,CUST_TYPE_CODE_2,CONSTITUTION_CODE,LEGAL_ENTITY_TYPE
FROM GENERAL_MASTER_TABLE where report_date = '30-JUN-2023' AND     constitution_code in ('11507', '11508', '11510', '11511', '11512', '11700', '22399', '22499', '33106', '33107', 'NBFC','NBFC ','11599',

  '24319', '24503','24337','13222') and SCHM_CODE IN ('CA101','CA102','CA103','CA106','CA107','CA108','CA109','CA110','CA111','CA112','LA101','LA106','OD001','OD002','OD003','OD028','OD651','SB105','SB107',
'TD115') and  ACT_BALANCE_AMT_LC>=0 ;

report_addl_criteria_1 = '0'

######################################################################################################

create or replace PROCEDURE BRF37B_DETAIL_PROCEDURE (REPORT_DATE DATE)
IS
  V_REPORT_DATE DATE := To_date (REPORT_DATE, 'DD-MM-YYYY'); 
   V_FROM_DATE dATE :=  ADD_MONTHS (LAST_DAY (REPORT_DATE), -1) + 1;
BEGIN


delete from BRF37B_DETAILTABLE where report_date = V_REPORT_DATE;
Commit;


insert into BRF37B_DETAILTABLE
( foracid, cust_id, ACCT_NAME,REPORT_DATE,ACT_BALANCE_AMT_LC, REPORT_LABLE_1,REPORT_NAME_1)
SELECT  foracid, cust_id, ACCT_NAME,REPORT_DATE,ACT_BALANCE_AMT_LC,REPORT_LABLE_1,REPORT_NAME_1 FROM 
brf37B_mapping_table where report_date = '30-JUN-2023' ;


COMMIT;


END;

create or replace procedure BRF37_BANKING_STATISTICS_PROCEDURE (Report_date VARCHAR2)
IS
----30-SEP-2020--
---VARARIBLE DECLARE
V_REPORT_DATE DATE := TO_DATE(Report_date,'DD-MM-YYYY');
V_REPORT_DUE_DATE DATE := Add_Months( Last_day (V_REPORT_DATE), +3);
V_REPORT_FROM_DATE DATE := Add_Months( Last_day (V_REPORT_DATE), -3)+1;

V_R11_DEMAND_DEPOSITS	varchar2(100 BYTE):='Demand Deposits';
V_R11_AED	Number(24,4):=0;
V_R11_FCY	Number(24,4):=0;
V_R11_TOTAL	Number(24,4):=0;
V_R11_COMMERCIAL	Number(24,4):=0;
V_R11_GRE	Number(24,4):=0;
V_R11_FDBI	Number(24,4):=0;
V_R11_SME	Number(24,4):=0;
V_R11_INDIVIDUAL	Number(24,4):=0;
V_R12_DEMAND_DEPOSITS1	varchar2(100 BYTE):='0';
V_R12_AED	Number(24,4):=0;
V_R12_FCY	Number(24,4):=0;
V_R12_TOTAL	Number(24,4):=0;
V_R12_COMMERCIAL	Number(24,4):=0;
V_R12_GRE	Number(24,4):=0;
V_R12_FDBI	Number(24,4):=0;
V_R12_SME	Number(24,4):=0;
V_R12_INDIVIDUAL	Number(24,4):=0;
V_R13_DEMAND_DEPOSITS2	varchar2(100 BYTE):='Above 0 to less than 2';
V_R13_AED	Number(24,4):=0;
V_R13_FCY	Number(24,4):=0;
V_R13_TOTAL	Number(24,4):=0;
V_R13_COMMERCIAL	Number(24,4):=0;
V_R13_GRE	Number(24,4):=0;
V_R13_FDBI	Number(24,4):=0;
V_R13_SME	Number(24,4):=0;
V_R13_INDIVIDUAL	Number(24,4):=0;
V_R14_DEMAND_DEPOSITS3	varchar2(100 BYTE):='From 2 to less than 4';
V_R14_AED	Number(24,4):=0;
V_R14_FCY	Number(24,4):=0;
V_R14_TOTAL	Number(24,4):=0;
V_R14_COMMERCIAL	Number(24,4):=0;
V_R14_GRE	Number(24,4):=0;
V_R14_FDBI	Number(24,4):=0;
V_R14_SME	Number(24,4):=0;
V_R14_INDIVIDUAL	Number(24,4):=0;
V_R15_DEMAND_DEPOSITS4	varchar2(100 BYTE):='From 4 and above';
V_R15_AED	Number(24,4):=0;
V_R15_FCY	Number(24,4):=0;
V_R15_TOTAL	Number(24,4):=0;
V_R15_COMMERCIAL	Number(24,4):=0;
V_R15_GRE	Number(24,4):=0;
